You\u2019re intrigued. Your scientist is smart, funny, confident. Visions of Louis\u00a0de Broglie or\u00a0Rosalind Franklin putting on their safety glasses and lab coats to come to do experiments with you runs through your head..</span></p>\n</div>\n<div data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: white; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, 'Bitstream Charter', serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; margin-bottom: 24px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">\n<p><span data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: transparent; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: black; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">Who can blame you? Science is a sexy occupation.</span></p>\n</div>\n<div data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: white; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, 'Bitstream Charter', serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; margin-bottom: 24px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">\n<p><span data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: transparent; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: black; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">But scientists aren\u2019t like the bimbos you usually pick up at the bar. Nor are they the assholes you ladies continually fall for. No, scientists are different beings (which is why you\u2019re attracted to them in the first place), and you should realize \u2014 before jumping in \u2014 that this isn\u2019t going to be a run-of-the-mill, boring, lame relationship you\u2019re used to.</span></p>\n</div>\n<div data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: white; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, 'Bitstream Charter', serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; margin-bottom: 24px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">\n<p><span data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: transparent; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: black; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">Here\u2019s what you need to know:</span></p>\n</div>\n<p><!--more--></p>\n<div data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: #333333; margin-bottom: 24px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">\n<p><span data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: transparent; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: black; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\"><strong data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: transparent; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">1. \u00a0We can figure things out.</strong>\u00a0Understand, we\u2019re paid to dig deep, find the secrets and wade through bullshit. We can pick up on subtleties, so what you think you are hiding from us won\u2019t be hidden for long. Sure, we\u2019ll act surprised when you eventually tell us you failed freshman biology in college \u2014 but we already knew.</span></p>\n</div>\n<div data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: #333333; margin-bottom: 24px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">\n<p><span data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: transparent; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: black; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">We don\u2019t take shit from anyone, so don\u2019t lie to us or give a load of bullshit. We spend all day separating fact from fiction, listening to scientific supply sales reps and dealing with students\u2019 bullshit. If you make us do the same with you, you\u2019re just gonna piss us off. And don\u2019t think we\u2019ll be quiet about it. We\u2019ll respond with the vengeance of an science blogger railing against some researcher\u2019s recently-retracted paper \u2014 and we\u2019ll enjoy doing it.</span></p>\n</div>\n<div data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: #333333; margin-bottom: 24px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">\n<p><span data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: transparent; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: black; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">Just tell us the truth. We can handle it.</span></p>\n</div>\n<div data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: #333333; margin-bottom: 24px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">\n<p><span data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: transparent; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: black; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\"><strong data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: transparent; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">2. \u00a0At some point, you will be a topic.</strong>\u00a0For either a research project or blog post covering an area of research, something you\u2019ve done or said will be the motivation. Get over it. Consider it a compliment, even if we\u2019re arguing against you in print.</span></p>\n</div>\n<div data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: #333333; margin-bottom: 24px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">\n<p><span data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: transparent; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: black; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">Think about it: we live our lives doing and writing about science. If you\u2019re a part of our life, we\u2019re going to do science on or\u00a0scientifically\u00a0write about you, your thoughts or a subject springing from one of the two.</span></p>\n</div>\n<div data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: #333333; margin-bottom: 24px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">\n<p><span data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: transparent; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: black; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">Don\u2019t be upset when an argument against your adoration of homeopathy turns up on our blog. Our lives are never boring and each day is different.</span></p>\n</div>\n<div data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">\n<p><span data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: transparent; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">The fact that we\u2019re inquisitive means we\u2019ll listen to you. Even if it does seem like an interview, we\u2019re paying attention to what you have to say (see rule No. 1).</span></p>\n</div>\n<div data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">We\u2019ll write about you or your thoughts because you\u2019re an important part of our life and we care about you (see rule No. 2).</span></p>\n</div>\n<div data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">Our brains are a great resource. Ever go on a date with an attractive person and wind up wishing you hadn\u2019t because everything they say is just, well, stupid? That\u2019s not going to happen here (see rule No. 3).</span></p>\n</div>\n<div data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: #333333; margin-bottom: 24px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">\n<p><span data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: transparent; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: black; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">Yes, it may seem that we put the job ahead of you, but we\u2019re driven. You\u2019re not with that loser whose life is going nowhere and who\u2019s completely content being mediocre (see rule No. 4).</span></p>\n</div>\n<div data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: #333333; margin-bottom: 24px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">\n<p><span data-blogger-escaped-style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: transparent; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; border-bottom-width: 0px; border-color: initial; border-image: initial; border-left-width: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; border-style: initial; border-top-width: 0px; color: black; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;\">There you go, five things you should know before dating a scientist. Feel free to add to the list, point out where I\u2019ve missed something or leave a comment.</span></p>\n</div>\n"}, "modified": "2015-09-18T01:20:10", "date_gmt": "2012-01-21T05:13:10", "_links": {"wp:term": [{"href": "http://rationalwhimsy.com/wp-json/wp/v2/categories?post=34", "embeddable": true, "taxonomy": "category"}, {"href": "http://rationalwhimsy.com/wp-json/wp/v2/tags?post=34", "embeddable": true, "taxonomy": "post_tag"}], "curies": [{"href": "https://api.w.org/{rel}", "name": "wp", "templated": true}], "self": [{"href": "http://rationalwhimsy.com/wp-json/wp/v2/posts/34"}], "version-history": [{"href": "http://rationalwhimsy.com/wp-json/wp/v2/posts/34/revisions"}], "collection": [{"href": "http://rationalwhimsy.com/wp-json/wp/v2/posts"}], "wp:featuredmedia": [{"href": "http://rationalwhimsy.com/wp-json/wp/v2/media/35", "embeddable": true}], "replies": [{"href": "http://rationalwhimsy.com/wp-json/wp/v2/comments?post=34", "embeddable": true}], "author": [{"href": "http://rationalwhimsy.com/wp-json/wp/v2/users/1", "embeddable": true}], "wp:attachment": [{"href": "http://rationalwhimsy.com/wp-json/wp/v2/media?parent=34"}], "about": [{"href": "http://rationalwhimsy.com/wp-json/wp/v2/types/post"}]}, "excerpt": {"protected": false, "rendered": "<p>Courtesy of the blog, Journal of Are You Fucking Kidding, we have the 5 Things You Should Know Before Dating a Scientist: So, you\u2019ve been eyeing that smart, attractive scientist you\u2019re lucky enough to know personally. You\u2019re intrigued. Your scientist is smart, funny, confident. Visions of Louis\u00a0de Broglie or\u00a0Rosalind Franklin putting on their safety glasses [&hellip;]</p>\n"}, "categories": [1], "tags": [20, 21, 22, 16], "guid": {"rendered": "http://rationalwhimsy.com/?p=34"}, "id": 34, "title": {"rendered": "5 Things You Should Know Before Dating a Scientist"}, "comment_status": "open", "author": 1, "modified_gmt": "2015-09-18T01:20:10", "meta": [], "sticky": false, "slug": "5-things-you-should-know-before-dating-a-scientist", "template": "", "ping_status": "open"}, {"featured_media": 25, "format": "standard", "type": "post", "link": "http://rationalwhimsy.com/new-years-resolutions-2012/", "date": "2012-01-20T04:49:57", "content": {"protected": false, "rendered": "<p><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-BlcIjwXIfR4/UGYjmyK8pOI/AAAAAAAAAIk/JqryYHmbRU8/s1600/New-Years-Resolution.jpg\"><img class=\"alignright\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-BlcIjwXIfR4/UGYjmyK8pOI/AAAAAAAAAIk/JqryYHmbRU8/s320/New-Years-Resolution.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"320\" height=\"244\" border=\"0\" /></a>This past year has been definitely a year of expansion for me, and as such I have had a rapid expansion of goals. \u00a0I actually want to remember these, so I made myself a separate file and just listed essentially all of the things that I&#8217;d like to either accomplish fully, or make some damn good progress toward in the coming year. \u00a0I then remembered that I had started this blog and decided that I could put them up here, and maybe even add a little bit of explanation on each item.</p>\n<p>My view of New Year&#8217;s Resolutions might be somewhat different than most people&#8217;s. \u00a0The impression that I get is that most people make a resolution, and if they don&#8217;t hold to it then they feel like the scum of the Earth. \u00a0My way of thinking about resolutions is thus: they&#8217;re just a list of goals that I want to work toward. \u00a0If I don&#8217;t achieve them, then I don&#8217;t achieve them. \u00a0But, as long as I make progress toward these goals, I&#8217;m alright. \u00a0And, if I happen to actually accomplish any of these, then even better! \u00a0It means that I&#8217;ve managed to take an active role in improving my life, and there&#8217;s documented change! \u00a0Awesome!</p>\n<p>Anyway, here&#8217;s&#8230;.most of them (some are meant to remain private), in no particular order:</p>\n<p><!--more--></p>\n<ul>\n<li>Pass the UW Astronomy Qualifying Exam at the doctorate level. \u00a0(<b>this one is not a &#8220;work towards&#8221; goal, it&#8217;s one of those &#8220;if you don&#8217;t do this then you&#8217;re scum of the Earth&#8221; goals</b>)*</li>\n<li>Run a 5K race in under 20 minutes</li>\n<li>Memorize 2 capoeira routines of at least 30 movements</li>\n<li>At least one takedown per jogo (capoeira game)</li>\n<li>Control of my angular momentum when performing the armada and meia lua de compasso kicks**</li>\n<li>Straighten legs during capoeira movements (unless of course the movement requires bent legs)</li>\n<li>Be able to perform a back handspring and a back walk-over well</li>\n<li>Be able to perform A\u00fa Sem M\u00e3os <a href=\"http://unknowncapoeira.com/_/Au_sem_Maos.html\" data-blogger-escaped-target=\"_blank\">(example)</a></li>\n<li>Be able to perform Mariposa <a href=\"http://unknowncapoeira.com/_/Mariposa.html\" data-blogger-escaped-target=\"_blank\">(example)</a></li>\n<li>Be able to hold a bananeira (normal, fechado, open, walking position, from headstand, walking, one-handed fechado, one-handed open, both sides) for at least 10 seconds</li>\n<li>Increase endurance so that I can play at least 2 consecutive five-minute games</li>\n<li>Work on jogo de dentro so that I&#8217;m never more than 1.5 leg&#8217;s length&#8217;s away from my opponent***</li>\n<li>Practice with Manganga consistently****</li>\n<li>Get to New York for the Guerreiros batizado*****</li>\n<li>Visit other Capoeira schools once per month</li>\n<li>Become proficient at the berimbau</li>\n<li>Become proficient at the pandeiro</li>\n<li>Lock down the Samba rhythm on the pandeiro</li>\n<li>Lock down the Samba rhythm on the atabaque</li>\n<li>Become a regular berimbau player</li>\n<li>Be able to play the gunga for rodas</li>\n<li>Go bouldering at least once per month</li>\n<li>Samba at least once per week (either in class or on my own)</li>\n<li>Dive back into Portuguese as soon as the Qualifying Exam is over******</li>\n<li>Communicate with friends regularly</li>\n<li>Start on a first-author paper with minimal outside help</li>\n<li>Obtain RA funding for Spring quarter (non-TA)</li>\n<li>Obtain RA funding for beyond Spring quarter (non-TA)</li>\n<li>Settle on a dissertation subject area*******</li>\n<li>Coordinate and go on an observing run</li>\n<li>Read and understand at least one paper per week.\u00a0 Note,\u00a0it&#8217;ll probably take at least 5 read-throughs to begin to understand each one.</li>\n<li>Save at least $1,000.00 in the bank by next new years, AFTER having spent money on leisure stuff</li>\n<li>Give blood at least once (successfully! \u00a0Remember to drink water!)</li>\n<li>See a psychologist at least once this year********</li>\n<li>Put $100 from every check into the credit card</li>\n<li>Eat out less than 4 times per week (including lunch and dinner)</li>\n<li>Enunciate your words, especially when you get excited. \u00a0You sound like you don&#8217;t know how to speak english when you&#8217;re worked up about something.</li>\n<li>Become knowledgable about the Candomble Orishas and practices</li>\n<li>Less broken commitments</li>\n<li>Floss at least once per week</li>\n<li>Get a video camera for capoeira before Batizado.\u00a0 Doesn&#8217;t need to be terribly high quality or anything, but something that can take continuous footage and have a tripod would be nice.\u00a0 (ex: Flip UltraHD Video Camera, ~$160, $10 tripod)</li>\n</ul>\n<div class=\"p1\">\n<p>*\u00a0<i>Pass the UW Astronomy Qualifying Exam at the doctorate level. \u2013\u00a0</i>The University of Washington Astronomy Qualifying Exam is what is given to the graduate students at the end of their first and second years. \u00a0Essentially, it is a 6-hour exam (with one hour separating the first and second sets of 3 hours) testing two years of astronomy graduate coursework. \u00a0It&#8217;s essentially a rite of passage for those hoping to continue on to obtaining their doctorate. \u00a0When it&#8217;s taken after the first year, failure is expected, as it very well should be. \u00a0You&#8217;re being tested on two years of knowledge after only one year of instruction. \u00a0You are, though, expected to fail gracefully, hitting that first year of knowledge pretty solidly on the exam. \u00a0It is possible for people to pass the exam in the first year, and actually happened with one of the guys in my cohort. \u00a0Once it&#8217;s passed, it&#8217;s never taken again. \u00a0There is a lower-level pass, the master&#8217;s pass, but if you pass at this level you still have to take it again.</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"p1\">\n<p>After the second year, it is <b>strongly suggested</b> that you pass at the doctorate level. \u00a0It&#8217;s not the end of the world if you don&#8217;t, but it is severely disappointing, and really gets you a lot of unwanted looks of pity. \u00a0It also means that you only have one more shot, which adds to the stress of taking it a third time. \u00a0You can of course take it a third time, but if you don&#8217;t pass that third time, they hand you a master&#8217;s degree and then show you the door (I think. \u00a0To my knowledge, no one here has hit that third strike).</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"p1\">\n<p>**\u00a0<i>Control of my angular momentum when performing the armada and meia lua de compasso kicks \u2013\u00a0</i>These are two kicks in capoeira that require a lot of spinning. \u00a0<b>Armada</b>\u00a0makes you spin while standing up, and <b>compasso</b>\u00a0makes you spin while crouched. \u00a0As it currently stands, I can usually land solidly like I&#8217;m supposed to after each kick, buuuuuut every so often I do lose my balance when I finish and it&#8217;s because I&#8217;m spinning too hard to control my legs.</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"p1\">\n<p>***\u00a0<i>Work on jogo de dentro so that I&#8217;m never more than 1.5 leg&#8217;s lengths away from my opponent \u2013\u00a0</i>I find that the most interesting games to watch are when the two players are weaving in and out of each other&#8217;s spaces, and usually these are jogo de dentro type games. \u00a0I also want to just work on my low game in general.</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"p1\">\n<p>****\u00a0<i>Practice with Manganga consistently \u2013\u00a0</i>Mangang\u00e1 is this dude I met through two other angoleiros who&#8217;s really cool and offers angola classes at his school in south Seattle, the Seattle Capoeira Center <a href=\"http://seattlecapoeiracenter.com/\" data-blogger-escaped-target=\"_blank\">(here)</a>. \u00a0He had offered a promotion last month, where if any of his Facebook friends wanted to come and take a morning class from him, it&#8217;d be for free. \u00a0So, I went to one on a Wednesday, at 6:45 in the morning. \u00a0It was one of the tougher classes that I&#8217;ve been in, but I thoroughly enjoyed it. \u00a0He seemed to also enjoy my being there and extended to me an offer of joining him regularly, with personalized coaching! \u00a0I decided to take him up on his offer, so starting next week (it was supposed to be this week, but snow halted everything), I&#8217;ll be getting my ass kicked every Wednesday and Friday morning, alongside my Senzala practice on Tues, Thurs, and Saturdays. \u00a0I&#8217;ll probably also be keeping up practice on my own on Sundays and Mondays. \u00a0We&#8217;ll see how this turns out!</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"p1\">\n<p>*****\u00a0<i>Get to New York for the Guerreiros batizado \u2013\u00a0</i>When I first started capoeira (almost exactly two years ago), I started in New York, at Columbia University with <a href=\"http://capoeiraguerreiros.org/\" data-blogger-escaped-target=\"_blank\">Capoeira Guerreiros</a>. \u00a0I got my first corda (something like the belts in Karate) with them at my first Batizado (portuguese for &#8220;baptism&#8221;), 2+ months after I had originally began. \u00a0It was one of the most fun things that I had ever done. \u00a0Unfortunately, I moved to Seattle that August, and thus stopped practicing with Guerreiros. \u00a0They&#8217;ve had a couple batizados since then, and I haven&#8217;t been able to make any of them because I&#8217;m broke and cannot afford to fly back to NY. \u00a0I&#8217;d like to be able to make it back and see how everyone&#8217;s improved in the past two years, and maybe even show off a little for them too.</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"p1\">\n<p>******\u00a0<i>Dive back into Portuguese as soon as the Qualifying Exam is over \u2013\u00a0</i>As part of my desire to become a great capoeirista, I want to learn Portuguese, which is the language of the activity. \u00a0I actually started formally learning it last quarter with a great teacher, and even made a few friends in the class, but toward the end of the quarter it became increasingly demanding (as it very well should). \u00a0It was so demanding that it had become difficult to learn the language and keep up with my actual graduate responsibilities. \u00a0So, with much pain in my heart, I decided to discontinue it this quarter so that I could focus solidly on my work. \u00a0I&#8217;m not giving up on it though! \u00a0Once my classes are through, I&#8217;m diving back into it, head first!</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"p1\">\n<p>*******\u00a0<i>Settle on a dissertation subject area \u2013\u00a0</i>In astronomy, most people aren&#8217;t interested in every single thing that the field has to offer. \u00a0Some people like planets and planetary systems (not me), some people like stars (hell yeah!), some people like Milky Way structure (I can dig it), some people like extragalactic astronomy, and others like large-scale structure, amongst many other things beyond and between. \u00a0I know that I&#8217;m pretty heavily interested in stars, but I am no where close to narrowing my interests down to something that can serve as the basis of a dissertation. \u00a0There&#8217;s so much to do with stars, and I just have so much left to learn. \u00a0This year though, I&#8217;m sure that I can get towards something that I can continue to study for the next 4.5 years.</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"p1\">\n<p>********\u00a0<i>See a psychologist at least once this year \u2013\u00a0</i>There&#8217;s nothing that I think is expressly wrong with me mentally. \u00a0However, over the past few years I&#8217;ve been through a few things that have produced varying amounts of trauma, and I&#8217;ve wanted to talk it out with a mental health professional. \u00a0On top of that, I kinda just want to talk to someone who has no other connection to my life about me. \u00a0Someone who&#8217;s supposed to be objective, and just have them listen to my story. \u00a0We&#8217;ll see how well I stick to this one.</p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"p1\"></div>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n"}, "modified": "2015-09-18T01:20:05", "date_gmt": "2012-01-20T04:49:57", "_links": {"wp:term": [{"href": "comment_status": "open", "author": 1, "modified_gmt": "2015-09-18T01:20:05", "meta": [], "sticky": false, "slug": "new-years-resolutions-2012", "template": "", "ping_status": "open"}, {"featured_media": 30, "format": "standard", "type": "post", "link": "http://rationalwhimsy.com/weathering-the-terrible-seattle-snowstorm-of-2012/", "date": "2012-01-18T04:44:16", "content": {"protected": false, "rendered": "<p><i><img class=\"alignleft\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-uu_CO_LsBac/UGYjQO1W4DI/AAAAAAAAAIc/7Un3-vUtTDY/s320/snowstorm.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"240\" height=\"320\" border=\"0\" />Picture courtesy of one of my coworkers&#8217; facebook albums.</i></p>\n<p>So last night, I&#8217;m sitting in my office putting the finishing touches on one of my homework assignments, when one of my friends who also happens to be there late appears at my door. \u00a0She tells me that she was getting ready to go and spend time with her boyfriend and wait through the oncoming snow storm at home. \u00a0She went on about how there was supposed to be up to 14 inches of accumulation between midnight and the next midnight, and how I should probably get home so that I don&#8217;t get snowed in. \u00a0Now, because I was in my office late and completely absorbed by what I was doing, I was completely taken by surprise by this announcement of inclement weather. \u00a0It also didn&#8217;t help much that when I looked out of my window, the skies (of SEATTLE!!!) were <i>essentially\u00a0</i>clear, and not a single flake had fallen yet from the sky. \u00a0I gave her a quizzical look and a sarcastic &#8220;ok, yeah. \u00a0I&#8217;ll see you tomorrow then.&#8221; \u00a0So she left, I kept working, and at some point later on in the night I left to go to my own home.</p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<p><!--more--></p>\n<p>Now there was already some snow on the ground, but this had been from the weekend. \u00a0It couldn&#8217;t have been more than 3 inches that had accumulated, but even this much holds the ability to SHUT SEATTLE DOWN!!!11!1one!!1uno! \u00a0However, by this point in the night it had more or less been moved out of the street, and no new snow was falling onto the ground. \u00a0It was dumb cold though. \u00a0Anyway, I hopped on the next bus home and walked home from my stop. \u00a0I got home at around 10:30 pm and hung out with my girlfriend, periodically looking outside to see where this fabled blizzard was.</p>\n<p>When we woke up this morning, we saw that the &#8220;snowstorm&#8221; had indeed come. \u00a0A whole 4-8 inches! WOW! \u00a0Yeah, they cancelled all classes for the day due to what really amounts to no more than a heavy dusting. \u00a0I stayed home because I had no real burning desire to head down to my office only to do the same stuff I ended up doing here today, and slept in a wee bit later (like 9am) than I had originally intended (like 5:30 am).</p>\n<p>I decided to be a beacon of virtue in the world and help out my apartment manager, Alan, shovel the walkway in our residential complex out to the street. \u00a0I figured it&#8217;d be a nice thing to do, especially considering that he&#8217;s fairly advanced in age and walks with an oxygen pack, and he had done me a huge solid last week. \u00a0So, we coordinated by phone, rallied our forces, collected some shovels from the basement and got out there. \u00a0It couldn&#8217;t have taken more than 10 minutes to shovel the walkway out to the stairs, clean the stairs, clear the courtyard, and shovel all the way out to the street. This brilliant idea then entered my mind: &#8220;hey, Nick, check it out. \u00a0You have this shovel in your hand, and an entire to day to do literally whatever the hell you want. \u00a0Why don&#8217;t you try your hand at shoveling some walk ways for money! \u00a0You could charge like $10-20 and make a hefty sum by lunch!&#8221; I asked Alan for his shovel and his blessing, which he gave freely. \u00a0I then set off on what would be a very short and disappointing venture into independent employment (a sign of things to come?).</p>\n<p>I decided to turn down the nearest street and just go door-to-door. \u00a0You know, the old fashioned way. \u00a0First house I stop at, I ring the doorbell twice and wait, standing proudly with my shovel: my gateway to outrageous fortune. \u00a0A young dude answers the door and I give him my shpiel about shoveling his walkway, sidewalk, and driveway for $10. \u00a0As I&#8217;m giving my sales pitch, I look out at the walkway and start to feel pretty silly. \u00a0His walkway couldn&#8217;t have been more than 30 feet long, and remember the accumulation throughout Seattle is only about 4-6 inches. \u00a0In addition to that, when I&#8217;m done giving my pitch, he informs me that he already swept (SWEPT! \u00a0I&#8217;m carrying a damn shovel and he did the same job with a BROOM!) his pathways off earlier and will probably just go out and do it again later. \u00a0I nod, accept the brief defeat, wish him a good day, and go across the street to try at the next house. \u00a0For every subsequent house, the story is either similar, or is some other valid reason as to why my services were not needed. \u00a0Either they were young, not lazy, and could do it themselves, or they were older and had one of the young kids in the neighborhood do it for free.</p>\n<p>After about 15 minutes of consistent rejection, it occurred to me that my time was probably better spent in my apartment, catching up on work that I&#8217;m currently a week (or more) late on. \u00a0So, I dragged my sorry self back home and told Alan to give me a heads up if the snow builds up again and needed swift conquering.</p>\n<p>I then proceeded to be&#8230;mildly productive. \u00a0Knocked out a little bit of homework, graded some quizzes, entered those grades and homework grades into the grade book, sent out some emails for class, and listened to a bunch of podcasts on <a href=\"http://risk-show.com/\" data-blogger-escaped-target=\"_blank\">Risk</a>. \u00a0And then I decided to start a blog.</p>\n<p>Ah, winter&#8230;</p>\n"}, "modified":
